style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">On </span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">June&#160;30, 2020</span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, Acuity Brands, Inc. (&#8220;we,&#8221; &#8220;our,&#8221; &#8220;us,&#8221; &#8220;the Company,&#8221; or similar references) issued a press release containing information about our results of operations for our fiscal quarter ended </span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">May&#160;31, 2020</span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K, which is incorporated herein by reference. The information contained in this paragraph, as well as Exhibit 99.1 referenced herein, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 5.02. Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">On June 25, 2020, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of Acuity Brands, Inc. increased the size of the Board from eleven to twelve members and elected Laura O&#8217;Shaughnessy to the Board. Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy, whose term will expire at the next annual meeting of stockholders, was also appointed to the Governance and Audit</span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Committees. </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy, age 42, is co-founder of SocialCode, LLC (&#8220;SocialCode&#8221;), a technology company that manages digital and social advertising for leading consumer brands, and has served as its Chief Executive Officer since 2009.  Prior to that Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy oversaw business development and product strategy for the Slate Group, an online publisher, where she specialized in advertising product development and strategic partnerships. Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy serves on the board of directors of Vroom, Inc.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">There are no arrangements between Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy and any other person pursuant to which Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy was selected as a director. No family relationships exist between Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy and any of the Company&#8217;s directors or executive officers.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy&#8217;s husband serves as the Chief Executive Officer of Graham Holdings, Inc. (&#8220;Graham Holdings&#8221;), and her father is the Chairman of the Board of Graham Holdings. SocialCode, where Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy serves as Chief Executive Officer, is owned by Graham Holdings. The Company made arm&#8217;s length purchases in the ordinary course of approximately $1.85 million in fiscal year 2019 and approximately $108,000 during the current fiscal year from another business owned by Graham Holdings (the &#8220;Graham Subsidiary&#8221;). We ceased issuing new purchase orders to the Graham Subsidiary in the first month of our third fiscal quarter, and we do not expect to make purchases from the Graham Subsidiary in the future. The purchases from the Graham Subsidiary during each of the last three fiscal years represented substantially less than 1% of each of Graham Holdings&#8217; and the Company&#8217;s consolidated revenues. </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Other than the transactions described above, there are no other transactions to which the Company is or was a participant and in which Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy has a material interest subject to disclosure under Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy will participate in the standard non-employee director compensation arrangements described under &#8220;Compensation of Directors&#8221; in the Company&#8217;s 2019 proxy statement filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on November 22, 2019. In accordance with the standard compensation arrangements, the Board approved a one-time restricted stock award for Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy with a value of $20,000 under the Company&#8217;s Amended and Restated 2012 Omnibus Stock Incentive Compensation Plan. The stock award will vest ratably over three years.  Additionally, the Company has entered into its standard form of Indemnification Agreement with Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy that provides for the Company to indemnify directors against all expenses (as defined in the agreement), judgments, fines and amounts paid in settlement actually and reasonably incurred by a director and arising out of the director&#8217;s service. The Form of Indemnification Agreement, filed as Exhibit 10.1 to this Current Report on Form 8&#8209;K, was previously filed with the Commission in a Form 8-K on February 9, 2010 and is incorporated herein by reference. </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">On June 30, 2020, the Company issued a press release announcing the appointment of Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy. A copy of this press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.2 and is incorporated herein by reference.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 8.01. Other Events.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">On </span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">June&#160;25, 2020</span><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, the Board declared a quarterly dividend of $0.13 per share.  A copy of the related press release is attached as Exhibit 99.3 to this Current Report on Form 8-K, which is incorporated herein by reference.</span></div><div><br/></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"></hr><div><div style="line-height:120%;-sec-extract:summary;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div></div><div><br/></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&#160;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:4pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:4pt;">&#160;</span></div><div <div><a name="sE391574EC11B55BFA2F755F09105E56B"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-left:0px;text-indent:0px;line-height:normal;padding-top:10px;text-align:-moz-right;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;width:99.609375%;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;margin-left:auto;margin-right:0;"><tr><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td style="width:34%;"></td><td style="width:33%;"></td><td style="width:33%;"></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Press Release</font></div><div style="text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Exhibit 99.1</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:center;font-size:15pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:15pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;     Acuity Brands Reports Fiscal 2020 Third Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">ATLANTA, June 30, 2020 - Acuity Brands, Inc. (NYSE: AYI) (&#8220;Company&#8221;) today announced results for the third quarter ended on May 31, 2020. Third quarter net sales were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$776 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">18.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the prior-year period. Gross profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">42.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">170</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points compared with the prior-year period. Operating profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">10.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">200</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points and adjusted operating profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">13.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">80</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points compared with the prior-year period. Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.52</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased by </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">31.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and adjusted diluted EPS of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.94</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased by </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">23.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the prior-year period. For the nine months ended May 31, 2020, cash generated from operations of $378 million increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$66 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">21.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with the prior-year period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Neil Ashe, President and Chief Executive Officer of Acuity Brands, commented, &#8220;Our company performed well in this challenging market environment associated with the global COVID-19 pandemic. The combined strength of our go-to-market channels, product portfolio, and supply chain allowed us to effectively serve the needs of customers across many categories. Despite our lower revenues, we were able to expand gross margins and to generate cash through a combination of actions that we took both before and during the pandemic.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:26px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal 2020 Third Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Fiscal 2020 third quarter net sales of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$776 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">18.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the prior-year period due primarily to a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">20%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decrease in volume largely as a result of the negative impact on demand due to the COVID-19 pandemic, partially offset by the benefit from acquisitions of approximately </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. The change in product prices and mix of products sold was flat year over year as a favorable shift in sales channel mix was offset by overall lower pricing.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross profit for the third quarter of fiscal 2020 decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$56 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$328 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$384 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior-year period, due primarily to lower sales volume, partially offset by lower costs for certain inputs as well as the contributions from acquisitions. Fiscal 2020 third quarter gross profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">42.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">170</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points compared with the prior-year period&#8217;s gross profit margin. The improvement in gross profit margin was due primarily to lower costs for certain inputs, contributions from acquisitions, and favorable sales channel mix partially offset by lower average selling prices. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Selling, distribution, and administrative (&#8220;SD&amp;A&#8221;) expenses for the third quarter of fiscal 2020 totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$241 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$22 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or approximately </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">8.4%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with the prior-year period. The decrease in SD&amp;A expense in the third quarter was due primarily to decreased freight and commissions associated with lower sales volume along with a reduction in costs across multiple expense categories as the Company adjusted spending in response to the lower net sales. The decrease in SD&amp;A expenses was partially offset by the additional costs from recent acquisitions, including additional amortization of acquired intangibles, commissions, and employee costs. SD&amp;A expenses for the third quarter of fiscal 2020 were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">31.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">27.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales for the prior-year period. Adjusted SD&amp;A expenses for the third quarter of fiscal 2020 totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$223 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">28.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales) compared with The Company is powered by approximately 12,000 dedicated and talented associates. Visit us at </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#0000ff;text-decoration:underline;">www.acuitybrands.com</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#0000ff;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This news release includes the following non-Generally Accepted Accounting Principles (GAAP) financial measures: &#8220;adjusted gross profit,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted gross profit margin,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted SD&amp;A expenses,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted operating profit,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted operating profit margin,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted net income,&#8221; and &#8220;adjusted diluted EPS.&#8221; These non-GAAP financial measures are provided to enhance the reader's overall understanding of the Company's current financial performance and prospects for the future. Specifically, management believes that these non-GAAP measures provide useful information to investors by excluding or adjusting items for manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and including special charges for actions taken in response to reduced demand due to the COVID-19 pandemic, and associated with efforts to streamline the organization to integrate acquisitions. Management typically adjusts for these items for internal reviews of performance and uses the above non-GAAP measures for baseline comparative operational analysis, decision making, and other activities. Management believes these non-GAAP measures provide greater comparability and enhanced visibility into the Company&#8217;s results of operations as well as comparability with many of its peers, especially those companies focused more on technology and software. Non-GAAP financial measures included in this news release should be considered in addition to, and not as a substitute for or superior to, results prepared in accordance with GAAP. The most directly comparable GAAP measure for adjusted gross profit and adjusted gross profit margin is &#8220;gross profit&#8221; and &#8220;gross profit margin,&#8221; respectively, which includes the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies and acquisition-related items. The most directly comparable GAAP measure for adjusted SD&amp;A expenses and adjusted SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales is &#8220;SD&amp;A expenses&#8221; and &#8220;SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales,&#8221; which include amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and acquisition-related items. The most directly comparable GAAP measures for adjusted operating profit and adjusted operating profit margin are &#8220;operating profit&#8221; and &#8220;operating profit margin,&#8221; respectively, which include the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and special charges. The most directly comparable GAAP measures for adjusted net income and adjusted diluted EPS are &#8220;net income&#8221; and &#8220;diluted EPS,&#8221; respectively, which include the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and special charges. A reconciliation of each measure to the most directly comparable GAAP measure is available in this news release. The Company&#8217;s non-GAAP financial measures may not be comparable to similarly titled non-GAAP financial measures used by other companies, have limitations as an analytical tool, and should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for GAAP financial measures.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:26px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Information</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This release contains forward-looking statements, within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. (NYSE: AYI) (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced today that the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) approved an increase in the size of the Board from 11 to 12 members and elected Laura O&#8217;Shaughnessy as a Director for a term that will expire at the Company&#8217;s next annual meeting of stockholders.  </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Ms. O&#8217;Shaughnessy is the co-founder and Chief Executive Officer of SocialCode, LLC, a technology company that manages digital and social advertising for leading consumer brands. (NYSE: AYI) is a market-leading industrial technology company. We design, manufacture, and bring to market innovative products and services that make the world more brilliant, productive, and connected including building management systems, lighting, lighting controls, and location-aware applications.  Based in Atlanta, Georgia, with operations across North America, Europe, and Asia, we are powered by approximately 12,000 dedicated and talented associates. (NYSE: AYI; &#8220;Company&#8221;) today declared a quarterly dividend of 13 cents per share. The dividend is payable on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">August&#160;3, 2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to shareholders of record on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">July&#160;17, 2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:9px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">About Acuity Brands</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Acuity Brands, Inc. (NYSE: AYI)&#160;is the North American market leader and one of the world&#8217;s leading providers of lighting and building management solutions. With fiscal year 2019 net sales of&#160;$3.7 billion,&#160;Acuity Brands&#160;currently employs approximately 12,000 associates and is headquartered in&#160;Atlanta, Georgia&#160;with operations throughout&#160;North America, and in&#160;Europe&#160;and&#160;Asia. The Company&#8217;s products and solutions are sold under various brands, including Lithonia Lighting&#174;, Holophane&#174;, Aculux&#174;, A-Light&#8482;, American Electric Lighting&#174;, Antique Street Lamps&#8482;, Atrius&#174;, Cyclone&#8482;, DGLogik&#8482;, Distech Controls&#174;, DTL&#174;, eldoLED&#174;, Eureka&#174;, Gotham&#174;, Healthcare Lighting&#174;, Hydrel&#174;, Indy&#8482;, IOTA&#174;, Juno&#174;, Lucid&#174;, Luminaire LED&#8482;, Luminis&#174;, Mark Architectural Lighting&#8482;, nLight&#174;, Peerless&#174;, RELOC&#174; Wiring, ROAM&#174;, Sensor Switch&#174;, Sunoptics&#174; and Winona&#174; Lighting. Visit us at&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#0000ff;text-decoration:underline;">www.acuitybrands.com</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8203;.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">#     #     #</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Company Contact:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Pete Shannin</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Acuity Brands, Inc.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">(770) 860-2873</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div>	</div></body>
